actor InvuledMarine : DoomPlayer
{
  player.displayname "DoomMarine"
  player.startitem "Pistol"
  player.startitem "Fist"
  player.startitem "Backpack" 1
  //player.runhealth 33
  +DONTGIB
  gibhealth -99999999999999
  states
  {
  Spawn:
     PLAY A -1
     Loop
  See:
     PLAY A 7
     PLAY B 7 //A_SpawnItem("Player_Footsteps",0,0,0,0)
     PLAY C 7
     PLAY D 7 //A_SpawnItem("Player_Footsteps",0,0,0,0)
     goto spawn
  Missile:
     PLAY E 10
     Goto Spawn
  Melee:
     PLAY F 5 Bright
     PLAY E 10
     Goto Spawn
  Pain:   
     PLAY G 3
     PLAY G 9 A_Pain
     Goto Spawn
  Death:
     PLAY H 10
     PLAY I 10 A_PlayerScream
     PLAY J 10 A_NoBlocking
     PLAY KLM 10
     Play M 0 Acs_Execute(248,0,0)
     PLAY N -1
     stop
  }
}

ACTOR HaxMaster3000Pro : Weapon 11153
{
	Inventory.PickupMessage "Omfg I hack I use the HaxMaster3000Pro"
	Inventory.PickupSound "misc/w_pkup"
	Weapon.SelectionOrder 650
	Weapon.AmmoType "Spirits"
	Weapon.AmmoGive 12
	Weapon.AmmoUse 1
	AttackSound "weapons/unmaker"
	+EXTREMEDEATH
	States
	{
   	Spawn:
   	  DMFP A -1
   	  Loop
   	Ready:
   	  DFPR ABCB 4 A_WeaponReady
      	  DFPR  A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/GROWL")
      	  DFPR  A 10 A_WeaponReady
   	  Loop
   	Deselect:
   	  DFPR A 1 A_Lower
   	  LOOP
   	Select: 
          DFPR A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/DRAW")
   	  DFPR A 1 A_Raise
     	  Goto Select+1
     	Fire:
          DFPR DE 4
          DFPR F 7
          DFPR A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/demonfirepowerfire")
          DFPR G 7 BRIGHT A_FireCustomMissile("FirepowerSpreadNuker", 0, 1, 0, 0) 
          DFPR HIJ 3
          Goto Ready
	}
}

{
	Health 1200
	Radius 36
	Height 100
	Mass 1000
	Speed 10
	MeleeDamage 8
	PainChance 100
        scale 1.8
	MONSTER
	+FLOORCLIP
	SeeSound "imp/sight"
	PainSound "imp/pain"
	DeathSound "imp/death"
	ActiveSound "imp/active"
	MeleeSound "imp/melee"
	Translation "48:79=160:167"
	MissileType FlameBall
	Obituary "%o was exploded in to pieces by a gold imp."
	HitObituary "%o was slashed by a gold imp."
	States
	{

		TROO AB 8 A_Look
		Loop

	See:
		TROO AABBCCDD 2 A_Chase
		Loop

	Missile:
		TROO E 12 A_FaceTarget
                TROO F 8 A_FaceTarget
		TROO G 0 A_CustomMissile("FlameBall",40,0,15)
                TROO G 0 A_CustomMissile("FlameBall",40,0,0)
                TROO G 6 A_CustomMissile("FlameBall",40,0,-15)
		Goto See

	Pain:
		TROO H 2
		TROO H 2 A_Pain
		Goto See

	Death:
		TROO N 5
                FLBL A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/rocklx")
                FLBL A 0 A_CustomMissile("FlameBallD",80,0,0)
                FLBL A 0 A_CustomMissile("FlameBallD",80,0,180)
                TROO O 5 A_XScream
                FLBL A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/rocklx")
                FLBL A 0 A_CustomMissile("FlameBallD",80,0,45)
                FLBL A 0 A_CustomMissile("FlameBallD",80,0,225)
                TROO P 5
                FLBL A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/rocklx")
                FLBL A 0 A_CustomMissile("FlameBallD",80,0,90)
                FLBL A 0 A_CustomMissile("FlameBallD",80,0,270)
		TROO Q 5 A_NoBlocking
                FLBL A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/rocklx")
                FLBL A 0 A_CustomMissile("FlameBallD",80,0,135)
                FLBL A 0 A_CustomMissile("FlameBallD",80,0,315)
		TROO RST 5
                FLBL A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/rocklx")
                TROO T 0 A_Explode(64,128)
		TROO U -1
		Stop
	}
}

// Credits for the BattleLord's decorate code to VoltLock but downgraded by UnTrustable (no expanding or shrinking deaths needed)
// I toke it, because i didnt want to invent the wheel again. Remember, if VoltLock haven't done it, i would have done it myself, like
// the rest of the Duke Nukem 3D monsters.
actor BattleLord 3502
{
  obituary "%o was destroyed by the Battle Lord."
  health 4500
  radius 40
  height 110
  mass 5000
  speed 12
  painchance 16
  seesound "lord/sight"
  attacksound "chaingun/shoot"
  painsound "lord/pain"
  deathsound "lord/death"
  activesound "lord/active"
  MONSTER
  +FLOORCLIP
  scale 1.0
  decal bulletchip
  //damagefactor "Shrinker", 0.6
  //damagefactor "Expander", 1.0
  //damagefactor "AlienShrinker", 0.0
  //damagefactor "BattleLord", 0.0
  //damagefactor "Explosion", 0.5
  +QUICKTORETALIATE
  +BOSS
  +MISSILEMORE
  +MISSILEEVENMORE
  minmissilechance 1
  states
  {
  Spawn:
    BLRD A 0
    BLRD A 0 //Thing_ChangeTID(0,1000)
    BLRD AB 10 A_Look
    loop
  See:
    BLRD AABBCCDD 4 A_Chase
    loop
  Missile:
    BLRD E 0 A_Jump(128,"Grenade")
    TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("MuzzleFlashSmall",32,16,0)
    BLRD F 2 bright A_CustomBulletAttack(6.6, 0.0, 2, 3, "BattleLordPuff")
    BLRD E 3 A_CPosRefire
    goto Missile+1
  Grenade:  
    BLRD G 0 A_JumpIfCloser(256,"Missile")
    BLRD G 0 A_Jump(32,"GrenadeDud")
    BLRD G 15 A_FaceTarget
    BLRD G 0 A_FaceTarget
    BLRD A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("rpg/shoot")
    BLRD H 0 A_CustomMissile("BattleLordAttack",32,16,0,2,32)
    BLRD H 15 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("MuzzleFlashSmall",32,16,0)
    BLRD G 15 A_FaceTarget
    BLRD G 0 A_FaceTarget
    BLRD A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("rpg/shoot")
    BLRD H 0 A_CustomMissile("BattleLordAttack",32,16,0,2,32)
    BLRD H 15 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("MuzzleFlashSmall",32,16,0)
    BLRD G 15 A_FaceTarget
    BLRD G 0 A_FaceTarget
    BLRD A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("rpg/shoot")
    BLRD H 0 A_CustomMissile("BattleLordAttack",32,16,0,2,32)
    BLRD H 15 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("MuzzleFlashSmall",32,16,0)
    goto See
  GrenadeDud:  
    BLRD G 0 A_JumpIfCloser(256,"Missile")
    BLRD G 15 A_FaceTarget
    BLRD G 0 A_FaceTarget
    BLRD A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("rpg/shoot")
    BLRD H 0 A_CustomMissile("BattleLordAttackDud",32,16,0,2,32)
    BLRD H 15 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("MuzzleFlashSmall",32,16,0)
    BLRD G 15 A_FaceTarget
    BLRD G 0 A_FaceTarget
    BLRD A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("rpg/shoot")
    BLRD H 0 A_CustomMissile("BattleLordAttackDud",32,16,0,2,32)
    BLRD H 15 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("MuzzleFlashSmall",32,16,0)
    BLRD G 15 A_FaceTarget
    BLRD G 0 A_FaceTarget
    BLRD A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("rpg/shoot")
    BLRD H 0 A_CustomMissile("BattleLordAttackDud",32,16,0,2,32)
    BLRD H 15 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("MuzzleFlashSmall",32,16,0)
    goto See
  Pain:
    BLRD A 0
    BLRD E 10 A_Pain
    goto Missile
  Death:
    BLRD I 20 A_Scream
    BLRD J 10
    BLRD K 10 A_NoBlocking
    BLRD LM 10
    BLRD N -1 A_BossDeath
    stop
  }
}

ACTOR FireWand : Weapon 25000
{
   Inventory.PickupSound "misc/w_pkup"
   Inventory.PickupMessage "You got the Fire Wand!"
   Weapon.AmmoType "Ember"
   Weapon.AmmoGive 20
   Weapon.AmmoUse 1
   Scale .5
   States
   {
   Spawn:
      FWDW A -1
      Loop
   Ready:
      FWND A 1 A_WeaponReady
      Loop
   Deselect:
      FWND A 1 A_Lower
      Loop
   Select:
      FWND A 1 A_Raise
      Loop
   Fire:
      FWND A 3
      FWND B 0 A_GunFlash
      FWND B 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/firewand")
      FWND C 4 A_FireCustomMissile("FireShot",0,1,0,0)
      FWND C 5
      FWND A 3 A_ReFire
      Goto Ready
   Hold:
      FWND C 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/firewand")
      FWND C 4 A_FireCustomMissile("FireShot",0,1,0,0)
      Goto Ready
   }
}

{
  Obituary "%o was chilled by %k's Frost Fang"
  Radius 20
  Height 12
  Inventory.PickupMessage "Frost Fang"
  Weapon.SelectionOrder 500
  Weapon.AmmoType "FrostAmmo"
  Weapon.AmmoUse 1
  Weapon.AmmoGive 30
  Weapon.SisterWeapon "FrostFangPowered"
  States
  {
  Ready:
    FSTF B 0 A_PlaySoundEx("FrostFang/Loop", "SoundSlot7", 1)
    FSTF B 0 A_Jump(1, 2)
    FSTF B 1 A_WeaponReady
    Loop
    FSTF CCCCCCCCCCCCCCC 1 Bright A_WeaponReady
    FSTF CCCCCCCCCCCCCCC 1 Bright A_WeaponReady
    FSTF CCCCCCCCCCCCCCC 1 Bright A_WeaponReady
    Loop
  Select:
    FSTF B 0 A_PlaySound("FrostFang/Raise")
    FSTF B 1 A_Raise
    Goto Select+1
  Deselect:
    FSTF B 0 A_StopSoundEx("SoundSlot7")
    FSTF B 0 A_PlaySound("FrostFang/Lower")
    FSTF B 1 A_Lower
    Goto Deselect+2
  Fire:
    FSTF B 3 Bright
    FSTF C 4 Bright
    FSTF D 5 Bright
  Hold:
    FSTF E 0 Bright A_PlayWeaponSound("FrostFang/Fire1")
    FSTF E 0 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("FrostFangFog2", 16, 0, 32, 0.5, 0, Random(-0.5, 0.5), Random(-50, 50), 128)
    FSTF E 0 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("FrostFangFog2", 16, 0, 32, 0.5, 0, Random(-0.5, 0.5), Random(-50, 50), 128)
    FSTF E 0 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("FrostFangFog2", 16, 0, 32, 0.5, 0, Random(-0.5, 0.5), Random(-50, 50), 128)
    FSTF E 0 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("FrostFangFog2", 16, 0, 32, 0.5, 0, Random(-0.5, 0.5), Random(-50, 50), 128)
    FSTF E 2 Bright A_FireCustomMissile("FrostFangShard", 0, 1, Random(-5, 5), Random(-5, 5))
    FSTF D 3 Bright A_Jump(12, 3)
    FSTF C 5 Bright A_ReFire
    FSTF B 4 Bright
    Goto Ready
    FSTF D 12 Bright
    FSTF C 5 Bright A_ReFire
    FSTF B 4 Bright
    Goto Ready
  Spawn:
    FSTF A -1
    Loop
   }
}

    goto See
  }

actor SSMachinegun : Weapon 10300
{
  //$CATEGORY UntSpawners
  attacksound "WolfMachinegunShot"
  decal BulletChip
  inventory.pickupsound "Wolf/Yeah"
  inventory.pickupmessage "You got the Machinegun!"
  inventory.icon "MCHGA0"
  weapon.selectionorder 400
  weapon.ammotype Magazine
  weapon.ammogive 20
  weapon.ammouse 1
  states
  {
  Spawn:
    MCHG A -1
    stop
  Ready:
    MCHF C 1 A_WeaponReady
    loop
  Deselect:
    MCHF C 1 A_Lower
    loop
  Select:
    MCHF C 1 A_Raise
    loop
  Fire:
    MCHF A 3 A_GunFlash
    MCHF B 3 A_FireBullets (2, 0, 2, 5, "BulletPuff")
    MCHF C 3 A_ReFire
    goto Ready
  Flash:
    MCHF A 3 bright A_Light1
    MCHF B 3 bright A_Light2
    MCHF C 3 A_Light0
    stop
  }
}
